<rate>4</rate>< Text>
Super great flavors.  We ordered the fried oysters and it came with Fries also and a side of their full house sauce to dip them in.  We ordered full house scallops, mussels, and shrimp.  Soooooo good.  We also ordered wings and chicken strips for the kids.  They really like it also and they came with fries which is nice, you don't have to get an extra side.  As you can see from the picture the sauce is packed with flavors and spices.   The scallops were nice and tender and the shrimp were perfectly cooked.  My only negative is that some of the mussels had some grit and broken shells...and about 5 of my mussels never opened.  I was scared to crack those open and eat them.  So I feel like that is a bit of a waste.  Other than that it was all awesome.</Text>

< Text>
This place is relatively small. Like most establishments in the same line. People were pleasant. Service was fine. At first glance, the price is noticeably less expensive than other places ie: Boiling Crab, Cajun Crab, Kinckin Crab etc. The huge surprise came when we received our food. 3 individuals each order their own pound of shrimp. It was then, I realized why the prices seemed to inexpensive. We received what looked like HALF a pound of actual shrimp. That‚Äôs when the waitress stayed ‚ÄúIt says on the menu, the pound includes the weight of the sauce aka: liquid.
I immediately looked at the menu and noticed the phrase, ‚ÄúAll seafood bags include sauce weight.‚Äù
Now, albeit my fault for not looking and reading the disclosure. But you can not deny that it is obviously masked within the text to be glossed over. AND. What other establishment ie: the examples provided above, include the weight of the sauce!?!?
It‚Äôs absurd and obviously a ploy to deceive their customers.
Definitely the first and last time we will visit this place.
AND. The flavor? Each individual agreed that they tasted their requested flavor and spice level for about 5 minutes. And then it dissipates and each of us ONLY taste butter. 2/10 on flavor.
Overall. 2/10. Just go somewhere which is more established and not going to try and con you.<//Text>

<review>Very strange McDonalds. It is attached to a gas station where you can enter through the gas station door or the McDonald's door and end up in the same space. It's not one of those places that has a very good parking lot. In fact when I first came here I actually thought it was a drive through because I didn't see any parking spaces for McDonald's patrons to park. Just before heading out, I finally found approximately 10 spaces tuck into the far corner by the drive-thru that didn't appear to belong to the gas station. Because of their they are pretty difficult to get into, and almost impossible to get out of.
The entire place is really not that clean. I have been here almost an hour and in that time no one has cleaned any of the tables or cleaned the garbage off of the floors.
They do have a pretty steady clientele mostly the drive-thru but many that walk in. Their menu seems complete. Prices are about the same across the board as other McDonald's I have visited. Yes, they do have high chairs!
The personnel seemed extremely pleasant. They tend to talk to each other well, get the job done and in a reasonable time. This is truly a fast food restaurant, the wait here is very short.
If you're looking for quiet, this is not the place to come. There's a lot of noise that comes from the gas station part of the building, the road that runs right beside the building, the drive-through and just the traffic of McDonald's workers and patrons themself.
Would I come back here? Actually I would. There's nothing here that scares me off. I feel safe, I feel secure, and the food was McDonald's food. Isn't that what I walked in for?
